country_event = { 
	id = 5014
	title = "EVTNAME5014"
	desc = "EVTDESC5014"
	picture = COURT_eventPicture
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = { 
		government = monarchy
		NOT = { 
			adm = 2
		}
		has_regency = no
		OR = { 
			faction_in_power = FC_NO
			faction_in_power = FC_CL
			faction_in_power = FC_BG
			faction_in_power = FC_BU
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = { 
		days = 1
	}
	option = { 
		name = "EVTOPTA5014"
		trigger = { 
			NOT = { 
				mil = 2

		}

			factor = 50
			modifier = { 
				factor = 2
				national_focus = MIL
			}
		}

		add_mil_power = 25
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				faction_in_power = FC_NO
			}

			hidden_effect = { 
				set_variable = { 
					which = opz

country_event = { 
	id = 5051
	title = "EVTNAME5051"
	desc = "EVTDESC5051"
	picture = ANGRY_MOB_eventPicture
	goto = uppity_artisans_province
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = { 
		any_owned_province = { 
			NOT = { 
				AND = { 
					check_variable = { 
						which = bcr
						value = 1
					}
				}
			}
			OR = { 
				has_province_modifier = PN_Minor
				has_province_modifier = PN_Important
				has_province_modifier = PN_Major
				has_province_modifier = PN_Dominant
			}
		}
		num_of_cities = 5
		NOT = { 
			stability = 3
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = { 
		days = 1
	}
	immediate = { 
		hidden_effect = { 
			random_owned_province = { 
				limit = { 
					NOT = { 
						AND = { 
							check_variable = { 
								which = bcr
								value = 1
							}
						}
					}
					OR = { 
						has_province_modifier = PN_Minor
						has_province_modifier = PN_Important
						has_province_modifier = PN_Major
						has_province_modifier = PN_Dominant
					}
				}
				save_event_target_as = uppity_artisans_province
			}
		}
	}
	option = { 
		name = "EVTOPTA5051"
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 25
			modifier = { 
				factor = 0.5
				NOT = { 
					stability = 1
				}
			}
			modifier = { 
				factor = 0.1
				NOT = { 
					stability = 0
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { 
			change_variable = { 
				which = ahf
				value = -300
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					AND = { 
						check_variable = { 
							which = ahf
							value = 1200
						}
					}
				}
				if = { 
					limit = { 
						stability = 3
					}
					set_variable = { 
						which = ahf
						value = 1200
					}
				}
				else = { 
					subtract_variable = { 
						which = ahf
						value = 1200
					}
					add_stability = 1
				}
			}
			else_if = { 
				limit = { 
					NOT = { 
						AND = { 
							check_variable = { 
								which = ahf
								value = 0
							}
						}
					}
				}
				if = { 
					limit = { 
						NOT = { 
							stability = -2
						}
					}
					set_variable = { 
						which = ahf
						value = 0
					}
				}
				else = { 
					change_variable = { 
						which = ahf
						value = 1200
					}
					add_stability = -1
				}
			}
			set_variable = { 
				which = ahd
				which = ahf
			}
			divide_variable = { 
				which = ahd
				value = 12
			}
			multiply_variable = { 
				which = ahd
				value = 0.1
			}
			multiply_variable = { 
				which = ahd
				value = 10
			}
			set_variable = { 
				which = lsc
				value = 100
			}
			subtract_variable = { 
				which = lsc
				which = ahd
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = POP_StabSubtract25
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				is_emperor_of_china = yes
			}
			add_mandate = -1
		}
		event_target:uppity_artisans_province = { 
			spawn_rebels = { 
				type = mob_rebels
				size = 0.5
			}
		}
	}
	option = { 
		name = "EVTOPTB5051"
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 75
			modifier = { 
				factor = 0.1
				NOT = { 
					treasury = 50
				}
			}
		}
		add_treasury = -50
		event_target:uppity_artisans_province = { 
			change_variable = { 
				which = aak
				value = 50
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					NOT = { 
						AND = { 
							check_variable = { 
								which = aak
								value = 1.0
							}
						}
					}
				}
				set_variable = { 
					which = aak
					value = 1.0
				}
			}
			set_province_flag = POP_ChangedWealth
		}
	}
	option = { 
		name = "personality_options.5051.a"
		highlight = yes
		trigger = { 
			ruler_has_personality = cruel_personality
		}
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 100
			modifier = { 
				factor = 0.1
				is_at_war = yes
			}
		}
		event_target:uppity_artisans_province = { 
			spawn_rebels = { 
				type = mob_rebels
				size = 0.5
			}
		}
	}
	option = { 
		name = "personality_options.5051.b"
		highlight = yes
		trigger = { 
			ruler_has_personality_ancestor = { 
				key = entrepreneur
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 100
		}
		add_adm_power = -25
	}
	option = { 
		name = "personality_options.5051.c"
		highlight = yes
		trigger = { 
			ruler_has_personality = obsessive_perfectionist_personality
		}
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 100
		}
		event_target:uppity_artisans_province = { 
			add_unrest = 10
		}
	}
}
